                        <script type="text/javascript">
                            var userbar = $('.userbar-switcher'),
                            actionbar = $('.action-bars__user-tools');

                            jQuery(function() {
                                wsSubscribe("auth:79856043.1581887389.89898b9da84fa2df57758611072ef62c7dd2e9de");

                                $('<audio id="chatAudio"><source src="/images/common/notify.ogg" type="audio/ogg"><source src="/images/common/notify.mp3" type="audio/mpeg"><source src="/images/common/notify.wav" type="audio/wav"></audio>').appendTo('body');

                                wsRegisterHandler("webnotify", function(data) {
                                    webnotify(data);
                                });

                                wsRegisterHandler("webnotify_bets_go", function(data) {
                                    webnotify(data);
                                });

                                wsRegisterHandler("moneybets", function(data) {
                                    $(".sys-userwallet").html(data);
                                });
                            });

                            function webnotify(data){
                                data = JSON.parse(data);
                                data.click = false;
                                data.iconUrl = '/images/logo_go.png';
                                if(data.url){
                                    data.click = function(){
                                        var win = window.open(data.url, '_blank');
                                        win.focus();
                                    };
                                }

                                data.open = function() {
                                    //console.log('Уведомление показано :-)');
                                };

                                jQuery.jGrowl(data.text, {
                                    sticky: true,
                                    position: "bottom-right",
                                    themeState: "highlight",
                                    click: data.click,
                                    open: data.open,
                                });
                              $('#chatAudio')[0].play();
                            }
                        </script>

<script>
    $(function() {
        $('.user-timezone-dropdown').baron({
            root: '.baron',
            scroller: '.baron__scroller',
            bar: '.baron__bar',
            scrollingCls: '_scrolling',
            draggingCls: '_dragging'
        });
        $('.user-timezone').on('click', function(){
            if($(this).hasClass('active')){
                $parentDiv = $('.user-timezone-dropdown .baron__scroller');
                $innerListItem = $('.user-timezone-dropdown-item.active');
                $parentDiv.scrollTop($parentDiv.scrollTop() + $innerListItem.position().top
                    - $parentDiv.height()/2 + $innerListItem.height()/2);
            }
        });
    });

    $('.ui-controller').on('click', function(e){
        controller($(this));
        return false;
    });

    $('body').on('click', function(e) {
        $('.ui-controller, .projects__items, .hamburger_projects-switcher-js, .userbar-user, .action-bars__user-tools, .userbar-user__bars, .hamburger_userbar-user-switcher-js, .change-lang__lang-items').removeClass('active');
    });

    function controller(dataNav){
        var domElements = dataNav.data();
        $(domElements.remove).removeClass('active');
        dataNav.add($(domElements.target)).stop().toggleClass('active');
    }

    window.onscroll = function(){
        var offsetTop = window.pageYOffset,
            headerHeight = $('.header__bottom').height(),
            headerElems = $('.logo, .header__projects');

        if(offsetTop >= headerHeight){
            headerElems.addClass('active');
        } else {
            headerElems.removeClass('active');
        }
    };
</script>        </div>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function(){
                    wsRegisterHandler("steamFriends", function(data) {
                if (!data.length) {
                    $(".sys-steam_friends_block").remove();
                    return;
                }

                $(".sys-steam_friends_list").html("").hide();
                $(".sys-steam_friends_count").html(data.length);

                for (var i = 0; i<data.length; i++) {
                    $(".sys-steam_friends_list").append(' \
                        <div class="steam-friends__item"> \
                            <a href="http://steamcommunity.com/profiles/'+data[i][0]+'" class="steam-friends__item-img tooltip" title="'+data[i][1]+'" > \
                                <img src="'+data[i][2]+'" alt=""> \
                            </a> \
                        </div> \
                    ');
                }

                if (data.length < 5) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < 5 - data.length; i++) {
                        $(".sys-steam_friends_list").append(' \
                            <div class="steam-friends__item"> \
                                <div class="steam-friends__item-img"> \
                                </div> \
                            </div> \
                        ');
                    }
                }

                $(".sys-steam_friends_block").addClass("loaded");
                $(".sys-steam_friends_counter").html(data.length);
                $('.sys-steam_friends_block .tooltip').tooltipster();
                $(".sys-steam_friends_list").owlCarousel({
                    nav: true,
                    dots: false,
                    items: 5,
                    loop: true,
                    slideBy: 'page',
                    navSpeed: 100,
                    mouseDrag: false
                });
                $(".sys-steam_friends_list").show();
            });

        $(".sys-steam_friends_list").owlCarousel({
            nav: true,
            dots: false,
            items: 5,
            loop: true,
            slideBy: 'page',
            navSpeed: 100,
            mouseDrag: false
        });

        $('.sys-steam_friends_block .tooltip').tooltipster();
    });
</script>

<script type="text/html" id="tmpl_livebet">
    {{live = it.live; }}

    <div class="bet-events__item">
        <div class="bet-event {{? live.my_bet_value_a > 0}}bet-left{{?}} {{? live.my_bet_value_b > 0}}bet-right{{?}} {{= bettingStatusIndex(it.m_status)}}" data-live-id="{{= live.m_id}}">
            /* Левая ставка */
            <div class="bet-event__user-bet bet-event__user-bet_left">
                <div class="user-bet">
                    <div class="user-bet__wrapper sys-close-bet">
                        <div class="user-bet__price-prize">
                            <div class="user-bet__price bet-currency bet-currency_{{= live.my_bet_currency}} sys-bet-user-summ-1">{{= numberWithSpaces(live.my_bet_value_a/100)}}</div>
                            <div class="user-bet__prize sys-bet-user-earn-summ-1">
                                + <span class="bet-currency bet-currency_{{= live.my_bet_currency?live.my_bet_currency:it.user_currency}}">{{= numberWithSpaces(parseFloat((live.my_bet_earn_a-live.my_bet_value_a)/100).toFixed(2) )}}</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="user-bet__team">{{= it.t1name}}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            /* Правая ставка */
            <div class="bet-event__user-bet bet-event__user-bet_right">
                <div class="user-bet">
                    <div class="user-bet__wrapper sys-close-bet">
                        <div class="user-bet__price-prize">
                            <div class="user-bet__price bet-currency bet-currency_{{= live.my_bet_currency}} sys-bet-user-summ-2">{{= numberWithSpaces(live.my_bet_value_b/100)}}</div>
                            <div class="user-bet__prize sys-bet-user-earn-summ-2">
                                + <span class="bet-currency bet-currency_{{= live.my_bet_currency?live.my_bet_currency:it.user_currency}}">{{= numberWithSpaces(parseFloat((live.my_bet_earn_b-live.my_bet_value_b)/100).toFixed(2) )}}</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="user-bet__team">{{= it.t2name}}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            <div class="bet-event__team bet-team bet-team_left">

<script type="text/javascript">

    function findMatch(id){
        return $.grep(_bets.bets, function(e){ return e.m_id == id; })[0];
    }

    function findChildes(id) {
        var result = [], key;
        for (key in _bets.bets) {
            if (_bets.bets[key]['m_parent'] == id) {
                result.push(_bets.bets[key]);
            }
        }

        return result;
    }

    var _bets = {
        bets : [],
        lowPriorityEnabled: false,
        lowPriorityCounter: 0,
        active_express: [],
        populateBets: function(bets) {
            var self = this;

            bets.forEach(function(b) {
                var bet = normalizeBet(b);

                bet.m_bets_a = 0;
                bet.m_bets_b = 0;

                // дополним инфу по картам
                var parent = null;
                if (bet.m_mapof) {
                    parent = bets.filter(function(e){return e.m_id == bet.m_mapof})[0];

                    if (bet.m_live_enable) {
                        parent.live_morphing = bet.m_id;
                        parent.m_koef_live_a = bet.m_koef_live_a;
                        parent.m_koef_live_b = bet.m_koef_live_b;
                        parent.m_koef_live_update = bet.m_koef_live_update;
                        parent.m_live_enable = bet.m_live_enable;
                        parent.locked        = bet.locked;

                        parent.live_restriction_a = bet.live_restriction_a;
                        parent.live_restriction_b = bet.live_restriction_b;
                    }
                }
                else if (bet.m_parent) {
                    parent = bets.filter(function(e){return e.m_id == bet.m_parent})[0];
                }

                if (parent) {
                    bet.t1name = parent.t1name;
                    bet.t2name = parent.t2name;
                    bet.t1logo = parent.t1logo;
                    bet.t2logo = parent.t2logo;
                    bet.l_name = parent.l_name;
                    bet.m_bo   = parent.m_bo;
                    bet.m_time = parent.m_time;
                }

                bet['live_restriction_'+USER_CURRENCY] = [0,0];

                if (bet.m_status == 0) {
                    reCalcSumBets(bet);
                } else {
                    if (typeof bet.sumbets !== "undefined" && typeof bet.sumbets[USER_CURRENCY] !== "undefined") {
                        bet.m_bets_a = parseInt(bet.sumbets[USER_CURRENCY][1] || 0, 10);
                        bet.m_bets_b = parseInt(bet.sumbets[USER_CURRENCY][2] || 0, 10);
                    }
                }

                var minBetValue = 100000;
                if (USER_CURRENCY !== 'RUB') {
                    minBetValue = minBetValue * currency_rates['RUB2' + USER_CURRENCY];
                }
                if (bet.m_status == 5 && bet.m_bets_a + bet.m_bets_b < minBetValue)
                    return;


                bet.user_currency = USER_CURRENCY;
                bet.stream = normalizeBetStreams(bet.m_stream);

                Object.observe(bet, betIndexObserver);

                self.bets.push(bet);
            });

            var future_count = self.bets.filter( function( element ) {
                return element.m_status == 0 && element.m_parent == 0;
            }).length;

            self.bets.forEach(function(bet){
                if (bet.m_parent || bet.m_mapof)
                    return;

                bet.childs = findChildes(bet.m_id);

                if (bet.m_status == 0 && _dt.timestampLeft(bet.m_time) < DOPS_OPENING_TIMEOUT && _bets.expenciveTouch(bet)) {
                    bet.touched = true;
                }

                if (future_count > 10 && _bets.lowPriorityEnabled) {
                    if (bet.m_status == 0 && _dt.timestampLeft(bet.m_time) > MAIN_OPENING_TIMEOUT && (bet.t1position >= 30 || !bet.t1position) && (bet.t2position >= 30 || !bet.t2position)) {
                        if (future_count - _bets.lowPriorityCounter < 10) {
                            return true;
                        }
                        bet.lowPriority = true;
                        _bets.lowPriorityCounter++;
                    }
                }
            });

            return this;
        },

        renderBets: function() {
            this.bets.forEach(function(bet){

                if (bet.m_parent || bet.m_mapof)
                    return;

                if (isExpressMode() && (!bet.m_koef_a || !bet.m_koef_b || (bet.m_status == 0 && _dt.timestampLeft(bet.m_koef_update) < -60000)))
                    return;

                if (isHistoryMode() && bet.m_status <= 1)
                    return;

                if (!isHistoryMode() && bet.m_status > 1)
                    return;

                _bets.createNewBlock(bet, ((bet.m_status == 0) ? 'prepend' : false));
            });

            this.handleNoActiveMessage();
            return this;
        },

        createNewBlock: function(bet, prepend) {
            if (bet.m_status == 0)
                $(".sys-games-next").tmpl('betsmatch', bet, prepend);
            else if (bet.m_status == 1)
                $(".sys-games-live").tmpl('betsmatch', bet, prepend);
            else
                $(".sys-games-past").tmpl('betsmatch', bet, prepend);
        },

        handleNoActiveMessage: function() {
            var nomatches = $('<div class="bet-items__not-items sys-no-active-matches"><div class="bet-items__not-items-text">Нет активных матчей</div></div>');

            var live = $(".sys-games-live");
            var next = $(".sys-games-next");

            if (!live.children().length) {
                live.append(nomatches.clone());
            } else {
                live.find(".sys-no-active-matches").remove();
            }

            if (!next.children().length) {
                next.append(function() {
                    var t = nomatches.clone();
                    t.find(".bet-items__not-items-text").text("Расписание уточняется");
                    return t;
                }());
            } else {
                next.find(".sys-no-active-matches").remove();
            }
        },

        renderActiveExpress: function(active_express) {
            this.active_express = active_express;

            if (active_express.length) {
                $('.sys-active-express-empty').hide();
            }

            active_express.forEach(function(e){
                e = normalizeBet(e);
                $(".sys-active-express-list").tmpl('activeExpress', e);
            });

            this.updateActiveExpressLength();
        },

        updateActiveExpressLength: function() {
            var expressActiveLength = $(".sys-express-active-length");
            if (!this.active_express.length) {
                expressActiveLength.hide();
            } else {
                expressActiveLength.show();
            }
            expressActiveLength.html(this.active_express.length);
        },

        closeAllGraphs: function() {
            $(".sys-graph-block:visible").slideUp(500, function() {
                $(this).html("").closest(".sys-betting").find(".sys-open-graph").removeClass("statloading");
            });
        },

        closeAllStreams: function(id){
            if (!id) id = -1;

            for (var b in this.bets) {
                if (this.bets[b].streamOpened && this.bets[b].m_id != id) {
                    $(".sys-betting[data-id="+this.bets[b].m_id+"]").find(".sys-open-stream").click();
                }
            }
        },

        expenciveTouch: function(bet) {
                        return (bet.m_bets_a+bet.m_bets_b > 100000000);
                    }
    };

    $(function() {

        _bets.renderActiveExpress([]);

        _bets.renderBets();

        if (_bets.lowPriorityCounter) {
            $(".sys-hidden-next-games-toggler-count").html(_bets.lowPriorityCounter);

            if (!isExpressMode()) {
                $(".sys-hidden-next-games-toggler").show();
            }
        }

        makeDialogAlive();

        if (typeof makeAgreementDialogAlive === 'function') {
            makeAgreementDialogAlive();
        }

        (function datetime_update() {
            for (key in _bets.bets) {

                var bet = _bets.bets[key];

                if (bet.m_parent > 0 || bet.m_mapof > 0 || bet.m_status > 1 )
                    continue;

                var block = $(".sys-betting[data-id="+bet['m_id']+"]");
                var timestamp = block.find(".sys-time-left").data('timestamp');

                if (bet.m_status == 0) {
                    block.find(".sys-time-left").html($.trim(_dt.timestampToLeftString(timestamp)));
                }

                // отрисуем иконку стрима, если матч стартовал или до начала меньше часа
                if (bet.stream && (_dt.timestampLeft(timestamp)/3600000 < 1 || bet.m_status === 1) ) {
                    block.addClass("bet-stream");
                }
                else {
                    block.removeClass("bet-stream");
                }

                if (!isExpressMode()) {

                    if (!block.hasClass("sys-betting-live") && isLiveEnabledForMatch(bet)) {
                        block.removeClass().addClass('bet-item sys-betting '+getClassesListForMatch(bet));
                        block.find(".sys-event-text-indside").html((bet.live_morphing !== 'undefined' && bet.live_morphing)?Lang('LIVE на карту')+" #"+findMatch(bet.live_morphing).m_mapindex:Lang('LIVE на матч'));
                        $("[data-parent-id="+bet.m_id+"]").tmpl('dop', $.extend({}, bet, {hideMatchId: true}), 'prepend');
                    }

                    if (block.hasClass("sys-betting-live") && !isLiveEnabledForMatch(bet) ) {
                        block.removeClass().addClass('bet-item sys-betting '+getClassesListForMatch(bet));
                        block.find(".sys-ordinar-holder-for-live").remove();
                    }
                }

                if (isExpressMode() && _dt.timestampLeft(bet.m_koef_update) < -60000 && block.length > 0 && bet.m_status == 0) {
                    block.slideUp('slow', function(block) {
                        block.remove();
                    }(block));
                }

                if (isExpressMode() && bet.m_koef_a && bet.m_koef_b && block.length == 0 && _dt.timestampLeft(bet.m_koef_update) > -60000 && bet.m_status == 0 ) {
                    $(".sys-games-next").tmpl('betsmatch', bet);
                    _bets.handleNoActiveMessage();
                }

                if (bet.m_status==0 && _dt.timestampLeft(bet.m_time) < DOPS_OPENING_TIMEOUT && _bets.expenciveTouch(bet) ) {
                    if (typeof bet.touched == 'undefined') {
                        block.replaceWith(renderedTmpl['#tmpl_betsmatch'](bet));
                        bet.touched = true;
                    }
                }

                if (bet.m_status == 0 && bet.lowPriority == true && _dt.timestampLeft(bet.m_time) < MAIN_OPENING_TIMEOUT) {
                    bet.lowPriority = false;
                    block.slideDown(300, function(){
                        $(this).addClass("bet-low-priority-opened");
                    });
                    _bets.lowPriorityCounter--;
                    if (_bets.lowPriorityCounter) {
                        $(".sys-hidden-next-games-toggler-count").html(_bets.lowPriorityCounter);
                    }
                    else {
                        $(".sys-hidden-next-games-toggler").hide();
                    }
                }
            }

            // У лайвов существует таймаут, чтобы часто не ставили. Если попап для ставки лайва открыт, и таймаут активен -- нам надо таймер обновлять
            var popup = $('.sys-bet-pop[data-live=true]:visible');
            if (popup.length) {
                var m = findMatch(popup.data("matchid"));

                if (typeof m.live_delay !== "undefined" && m.live_delay > new Date().getTime() + 1000 ) {
                    // если до конца таймаута более 1 секунды -- отрисовываем таймер
                    popup.find(".sys-btn-makebet").attr("disabled", true).html(parseInt((m.live_delay - new Date().getTime())/1000));
                }
                else if (typeof m.live_delay !== "undefined" && new Date().getTime() - m.live_delay < 2000 ) {
                    // таймаут завершился. сделаем кнопку ставки активной и с текстом
                    popup.find(".sys-btn-makebet").html("Сделать ставку");

                    btnMakebetValidate();
                }
            }

            setTimeout(datetime_update, 1000);
        })();

        $(".sys-betting:not(.bet-has-news) .sys-tourney-pic IMG").tooltipster({
            theme: 'tooltipster-borderless tooltipster-champ',
            delay: 100,
            side: 'right',
            distance: 0
        });

        $(".sys-betting.bet-has-news .sys-tourney-pic IMG").tooltipster({

        $(".sys-m-comment").tooltipster({

        $(document).on("click", ".sys-makebet-button", koefButtonHandler);

        $(document).on("click", ".sys-open-graph", function(){

            if ($(this).hasClass("statloading"))
                return;

            var block = $(this).closest(".sys-betting");
            var id    = block.data("id");
            var graph = block.find(".sys-graph-block");

            $(this).addClass("statloading");

            if (!graph.is(':visible')) {

                var load_url = RELATIVE_PATH+"graph/"+id+"/";

                $.ajax(load_url)
                    .done(function(data){
                        statistics = JSON.parse(data);

                        graph
                            .tmpl('statistics', {m: findMatch(id), compare: statistics.compare, lastMatches: statistics.lastMatches})
                            .append('<div id="bm-graph-'+id+'" style="width:100%; height: 450px; background: #3f3f4f; color:#ffffff;"></div>')
                            .slideDown(500, function(){
                                block.find(".sys-open-graph").removeClass("statloading");
                            });

                        BetsChart.initGraph('bm-graph-'+id, findMatch(id), statistics.graph);

                        $(".sys-teams-comparison-info").tooltipster({
                            theme: 'tooltipster-borderless',
                            delay: 100,
                            side: 'left',
                            distance: 5,
                            maxWidth: 230
                        });
                    })
                    .fail(function(){
                        block.find(".sys-open-graph").removeClass("statloading");
                    });
            }
            else {
                // все графики закрыты
                BetsChart.open_graph_id = 0;
            }

            _bets.closeAllGraphs();
        });

        $(document).on("click", ".sys-reopen-stream", function(){
            $e = $(this);
            var block = $e.closest(".sys-betting");
            block.find(".sys-player").html('');
            block.find(".sys-reopen-stream").removeClass('active');
            $e.addClass('active');
            block.find(".sys-player").tmpl('stream', $e.data('info'));
        });

        $(document).on("click", ".sys-open-stream", function(){
            var block = $(this).closest(".sys-betting");
            var id    = block.data("id");
            var bet   = findMatch(id);

            if (bet.streamOpened) {
                bet.streamOpened = false;

                block.find(".sys-open-stream").addClass("statloading");
                block.find(".sys-stream-block").slideUp(function(){
                    block.find(".sys-multistream").html('');
                    block.find(".sys-player").html('');
                    block.find(".sys-open-stream").removeClass("statloading");
                    if (!bet.stream)
                        block.find(".bet-match").removeClass("bet-stream");
                });
            } else if (bet.stream) {
                bet.streamOpened = true;
                bet.stream[0]['active'] = true;

                block.find(".sys-open-stream").addClass("statloading");
                if (bet.stream.length > 1) {
                    block.find(".sys-multistream").tmpl('multistream', bet.stream);
                }
                block.find(".sys-player").tmpl('stream', bet.stream[0]);
                block.find(".sys-stream-block").slideDown(500, function(){
                    block.find(".sys-open-stream").removeClass("statloading");
                });
            }
        });

        // attachHandler to dialog close button
        wsSubscribe("bets");

        WsEvents.cancelBet();

        WsEvents.placeBet();

        WsEvents.placeLiveBet();

        WsEvents.matchStatus();

        WsEvents.updateBets();

        wsRegisterHandler("newmatch_go", function(data) {
            if (data.m_parent || data.m_mapof) return;

            var bet = normalizeBet(data);
            bet.sumbets = {};
            bet.user_currency = USER_CURRENCY;
            bet.stream = normalizeBetStreams(bet.m_stream);

            Object.observe(bet, betIndexObserver);

            _bets.bets.push(bet);

            if (isExpressMode())
                return;

            _bets.createNewBlock(bet);
            _bets.handleNoActiveMessage();
        });

        WsEvents.updateMatch("go", _bets.active_express);

        WsEvents.currencyUpdate(_bets.bets);

        $(document).on('click', ".sys-matchlink", function(){
            $(this).addClass("statloading");
        });

        //////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        // крестик отмены ставки
        $(document).on("click", ".sys-close-bet", function() {
            var match = findMatch($(this).closest(".sys-betting").attr("data-id"));
            if (typeof match !== 'undefined' && match.m_status == 0)
                closeBet(match.m_id);
        });

        $(document).on("click", ".sys-hidden-next-games-toggler", function() {
            var lowBetItems = $(".bet-low-priority");
            if (lowBetItems.hasClass("bet-low-priority-opened")) {
                hideBetLowPriority(lowBetItems);
            } else {
                showBetLowPriority(lowBetItems);
            }
        });

        function showBetLowPriority(items) {
            $(".sys-hidden-next-games-text-showit").css("display","none");
            $(".sys-hidden-next-games-text-hideit").css("display","inline");
            items.slideToggle(0, function(){
                $(this).addClass("bet-low-priority-opened");
            });
        }

        function hideBetLowPriority(items) {
            $(".sys-hidden-next-games-text-showit").css("display","inline");
            $(".sys-hidden-next-games-text-hideit").css("display","none");
            items.slideToggle(300, function(){
                $(this).removeClass("bet-low-priority-opened");
            });
        }

        // toggle additional bets block
        $(document).on("click", ".sys-bet-additional-opener", function(e) {
            var id = $(e.target).closest(".sys-betting").data('id');
            var match = findMatch(id);
            match.touched = (match.touched)?false:true;
            $(e.target).closest(".sys-betting").toggleClass("bet-events-opened").find(".sys-events").toggle();
            return false;
        });
        $(document).on("click", ".sys-load-more-events", function(e) {
            var block = $(e.target).closest(".sys-betting");
            $(this).toggleClass("active");
            block.find(".sys-events-subcat").toggle();
            if ($(this).hasClass("active")) {
                $(e.target).html($(e.target).data("text2"));
            }
            else {
                $(e.target).html($(e.target).data("text1"));
            }
            return false;
        });

        $(document).on("click", ".sys-total-tab", function(){
            if ($(".sys-total-tab").hasClass("active"))
                return;

            if (_bets.lowPriorityCounter) {
                hideBetLowPriority($(".bet-low-priority"));
                $(".sys-hidden-next-games-toggler").slideDown();
            }

            $(".sys-tab").removeClass("active");
            $(".sys-expess-sidebar").hide();
            $(this).addClass("active");
            $(".sys-games").html('');
            $(".sys-bets-block").removeClass("express history").addClass("total");
            setCookie("page-tab", "1", 7);
            _bets.renderBets();
        });

        $(document).on("click", ".sys-express-tab", function(){
            if ($(".sys-express-tab").hasClass("active"))
                return;

            $(".sys-hidden-next-games-toggler").hide();

            $(".sys-tab").removeClass("active");
            $(".sys-expess-sidebar").show();
            $(this).addClass("active");
            $(".sys-games").html('');
            $(".sys-bets-block").removeClass("total history").addClass("express");
            setCookie("page-tab", "2", 7);
            _bets.renderBets();
        });

        $(document).on("click", ".sys-history-tab", function(){
            if ($(".sys-history-tab").hasClass("active"))
                return;

            $(".sys-hidden-next-games-toggler").hide();

            $(".sys-tab").removeClass("active");
            $(".sys-expess-sidebar").hide();
            $(this).addClass("active");
            $(".sys-games").html('');
            $(".sys-bets-block").removeClass("total express").addClass("history");
            setCookie("page-tab", "3", 7);
            _bets.renderBets();
        });

        makeExpressMenuAlive();
    });

</script>

$(document).ready(function(){
  CHAT = createChat(10);
  CHAT.isCanReported = true;
  CHAT.init($(".chat-place .chat"));
  CHAT.inlineInfo.hash = "e314a9f41c4ef8ff869863ed06fa2b70";
  CHAT.language = "ru";
});

function setChat(chatId, e) {
    if (chatId === chatID) {
        return false;
    }

    $.ajax({
        url: PATH+'chat/?action=setChat&chatid='+chatId.toString(),
        dataType: "JSON",
        cache: false
    }).done(function(data) {
        if (!data.success) {
            return;
        }

        wsUnSubscribe('chat' + chatID);
        wsReconnect();
        var reconnectInterval = setInterval(function() {
            if (!wsIsConnected()) {
                return false;
            }
            clearInterval(reconnectInterval);

            chatID = chatId;
            current_id = parseInt(data.min_id);
            CHAT.chat.html('');
            CHAT.initChatSocket(chatID);
            CHAT.appendMessages(data.messages.reverse() || []);
            CHAT.appendPinMessage(data.pin_message);
            CHAT.container.find('.baron__scroller').scrollTop(CHAT.container.find('.baron__scroller').innerHeight());

            var wrap = $('.sys-chat-langs');
            wrap.find('.chat-langs-item').removeClass('active');
            e.addClass('active');
        }, 100);
    }).fail(function(jqXHR, textStatus) {
        CHAT.chat.html("<center>Ошибка загрузки</center>" + CHAT.chat.html());
    }).always(function(){
        CHAT.sending = false;
        CHAT.container.find(".chat-loader").removeClass("active");
    });
}
</script>
